            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             string
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the string to reverse.
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->
        <div class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-github crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always" id="crayon-558b4d16d40b0526771171" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;" wrap="soft">

        <h2>
         61. addslashes()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           addslashes()
          </code>
          function returns a string with backslashes in front of predefined characters.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Returns escaped instances of characters in string by adding a backslash before them. You can specify ranges of characters by separating them with two periods; for example, to escape characters between b and o, use "b..o". Multiple characters and ranges can be specified in characters.
        </p>
        <h3>
         addslashes function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           addslashes
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           string
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             string
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the string to be escaped.
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>

         Code Example

        <h2>
         62. count_chars()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           count_chars()
          </code>
          function returns information about characters used in a string
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Returns the number of occurrences of each byte value from 0255 in
         <strong>
          string
         </strong>
         
         <strong>
          mode
         </strong>
         determines the form of the result.
        </p>
        <h3>
         count_chars function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           count_chars
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           string, mode
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             string
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Required. The string to be checked
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             mode
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. Specifies the return modes.   	0 is default. The different return modes are:
            <ul>
             <li>
              0  an array with the ASCII value as key and number of occurrences as value
             </li>
             <li>
              1  an array with the ASCII value as key and number of occurrences as value, only lists occurrences greater than zero
             </li>
             <li>
              2  an array with the ASCII value as key and number of occurrences as value, only lists occurrences equal to zero are listed
             </li>
             <li>
              3  a string with all the different characters used
             </li>
             <li>
              4  a string with all the unused characters
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->
        <div class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-github crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always" id="crayon-558b4d16d40bc810392232" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">

        <h2>
         63. md5_file()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           md5_file()
          </code>
          function calculates the MD5 hash of a file.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Calculates and returns the MD5 encryption hash for the file at
         <strong>
          file
         </strong>
         . An MD5 hash is a 32-character hexadecimal value that can be used to checksum a files data. If
         <strong>
          raw
         </strong>
         is supplied and is true, the result is sent as a 16-bit binary value instead.
        </p>
        <h3>
         md5_file function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           substr
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           file, raw
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             file
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. The file to be calculated
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             raw
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. A boolean value that specifies hex or binary output format:
            <ul>
             <li>
              TRUE  Raw 16 character binary format
             </li>
             <li>
              FALSE  Default. 32 character hex number
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

        <h2>
         64. nl2br()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           nl2br()
          </code>
          function inserts HTML line breaks (&lt;br&gt; or &lt;br /&gt;) in front   of each newline (n) in a string.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         If
         <strong>
          xhtml
         </strong>
         is true, then nl2br will use XHTML-compatible line breaks..
        </p>
        <h3>
         nl2br function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           nl2br
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           string, xhtml
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             string
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the string to check
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             xhtml
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. A boolean value that indicates whether or not to use XHTML compatible line breaks:
            <ul>
             <li>
              TRUE- Default. Inserts &lt;br /&gt;
             </li>
             <li>
              FALSE  Inserts &lt;br&gt;
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->
        <div class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-github crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always" id="crayon-558b4d16d40c7746054587" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;" wrap="soft">
           &lt;?php
echo nl2br("This is a piece of text on line 1.nYet this text is on line 2.");
?&gt;
          </textarea>
         </div>
         <div class="crayon-main" style="">
          <table class="crayon-table">
           <tr class="crayon-row">
            <td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="hide">
             <div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40c7746054587-1">
               1
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40c7746054587-2">
               2
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40c7746054587-3">
               3

        <hr/>
        <h2>
         65. sha1_file()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           sha1_file()
          </code>
          function calculates the SHA-1 hash of a file.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Calculates and returns the sha1 encryption hash for the file at
         <strong>
          file
         </strong>
         . A sha1 hash is a 40-character hexadecimal value that can be used to checksum a files data. If
         <strong>
          raw
         </strong>
         is supplied and is true, the result is sent as a 20-bit binary value instead.
        </p>
        <h3>
         sha1_file function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           sha1_file
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           file, raw
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             file
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. The file to be calculated
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             raw
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. A boolean value that specifies hex or binary output format:
            <ul>
             <li>
              TRUE  Raw 20 character binary format
             </li>
             <li>
              FALSE  Default. 40 character hex number
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

$sha1file = sha1_file($file);

        <hr/>
        <h2>
         66. str_word_count()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           str_word_count()
          </code>
          function returns a part of a string.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Counts the number of words in string using locale-specific rules. The value of
         <strong>
          return
         </strong>
         dictates the returned value.
        </p>
        <h3>
         str_word_count function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           str_word_count
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           string, return, char
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             string
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the string to check
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             return
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. Specifies the return value of the str_word_count() function.
            <p>
             Possible values:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              0  Default. Returns the number of words found
             </li>
             <li>
              1  Returns an array with the words from the string
             </li>
             <li>
              2  Returns an array where the key is the position of the word in the string, and value is the actual word
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             char
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. Specifies special characters to be considered as words.
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

        <h2>
         67. strnatcasecmp()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           strnatcasecmp()
          </code>
          function compares two strings using a natural order algorithm.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Compares two strings with case insensitivity and returns a number less than 0 if
         <strong>
          stringone
         </strong>
         is less than
         <strong>
          stringtwo
         </strong>
         , 0 if the two strings are equal, and a number greater than 0 if
         <strong>
          stringone
         </strong>
         is greater than
         <strong>
          stringtwo
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <h3>
         strnatcasecmp function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           strnatcasecmp
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           stringone, stringtwo
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             stringone
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the first string to compare
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             stringtwo
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the second string to compare
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;" wrap="soft">
           &lt;?php

    "file1",
    "file2",

    "file01",
    "file100",
    "file20",
    "file30",
    "file200"
);

usort($firstarray, "strcmp");
print_r($firstarray);
echo "&lt;br /&gt;";
echo "This uses the Natural Order" . "&lt;br /&gt;";

print_r($secondarray);

             This sort uses standard ordering
Array
(
    [0] =&gt; file01
    [1] =&gt; file1
    [2] =&gt; file10

                 <span class="crayon-sy">
                  )
                 </span>
                </div>
               </div>
              </td>
             </tr>
            </table>
           </div>
          </div>
          <!-- [Format Time: 0.0092 seconds] -->
          <br/>
         </strong>
        </div>
        <hr/>
        <h2>
         68. strnatcmp()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           strnatcmp()
          </code>
          function compares two strings using a natural order algorithm.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Compares two strings
         <em>
          with case sensitivity
         </em>
         and returns a number less than 0 if
         <strong>
          stringone
         </strong>
         is less than
         <strong>
          stringtwo
         </strong>
         , 0 if the two strings are equal, and a number greater than 0 if
         <strong>
          stringone
         </strong>
         is greater than
         <strong>
          stringtwo
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <h3>
         strnatcmp function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           strnatcmp
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           string,start,length
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             stringone
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the first string to compare
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             stringtwo
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the second string to compare
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->
        <div class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-github crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always" id="crayon-558b4d16d40e3888349445" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;" wrap="soft">
           &lt;?php
$firstarray = $secondarray = array(
    "FilE1",
    "fiLE2",
    "filE10",
    "fiLE01",
    "fILe100",
    "fIle20",
    "File30",
    "FIle200"
);
echo "This sort uses standard ordering" . "&lt;br /&gt;";
usort($firstarray, "strcmp");
print_r($firstarray);
echo "&lt;br /&gt;";
echo "This uses the Natural Order" . "&lt;br /&gt;";
usort($secondarray, "strnatcmp");
print_r($secondarray);
?&gt;

        <hr/>
        <h2>
         69. strncmp()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           strncmp()
          </code>
          function compares two strings.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         This function works just like
         <code>
          strcmp()
         </code>
         function, except that
         <code>
          strcmp()
         </code>
         does not have the length parameter.
        </p>
        <h3>
         strncmp function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           strncmp
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           stringone, stringtwo, length
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             stringone
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the first string to compare
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             stringtwo
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the second string to compare
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             length
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specify the number of characters from each string to be used in the comparison
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->
        <div class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-github crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always" id="crayon-558b4d16d40ef621227601" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;" wrap="soft">
           &lt;?php
$equal = strncmp("Awesome people do awesome things.", "Awesome birds fly fast.", 7);

$notequal = strncmp("Awesome people do awesome things.", "Awesome birds fly fast.", 9);

echo "Since $equal is equal, the value is $equal.  Since $notequal is not equal, the value is $notequal.";

?&gt;
          </textarea>
         </div>

        <hr/>
        <h2>
         70. chop()
         <small>
          <strong>
           definition:
          </strong>
          The
          <code>
           chop()
          </code>
          function removes whitespaces or other predefined characters   from the right end of a string.
         </small>
        </h2>
        <p>
         <span class="label label-info">
          <strong>
           Usage:
          </strong>
         </span>
         This works just like the
         <code>
          rtrim()
         </code>
         function.
        </p>
        <h3>
         chop function signature
         <small>
          <strong>
           chop
          </strong>
          (
          <em>
           string, charlist
          </em>
          )
         </small>
        </h3>
        <p>
        </p>
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover">
         <tbody>
          <tr>
           <th>
            Argument
           </th>
           <th>
            Argument Meaning
           </th>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             string
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Mandatory. Specifies the string to check
           </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
           <td>
            <em>
             charlist
            </em>
           </td>
           <td>
            Not Mandatory. Specifies which characters to remove from the string.
            <br/>
            The following characters are removed if the charlist parameter is empty:
            <ul>
             <li>
                NULL
             </li>
             <li>
              t  tab
             </li>
             <li>
              n  new line
             </li>
             <li>
              x0B  vertical tab
             </li>
             <li>
              r  carriage return
             </li>
             <li>
                 ordinary white space
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </tbody>
        </table>
        <h4>
         Code Example
        </h4>
        <p>
        </p>
        <!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->
        <div class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-github crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-always" id="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
         <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
          <textarea class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly="" style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;" wrap="soft">
           &lt;?php
$chopped = rtrim('You really are the most interesting person in the world. cANyOUbELIEVEtHAT?', 'cANyOUbELIEVEtHAT?');
echo $chopped;
?&gt;
          </textarea>
         </div>
         <div class="crayon-main" style="">
          <table class="crayon-table">
           <tr class="crayon-row">
            <td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="hide">
             <div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
              <div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-1">
               1
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-2">
               2
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-3">
               3
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-4">
               4
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
            <td class="crayon-code">
             <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 14px !important; line-height: 18px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
              <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-1">
               <span class="crayon-ta">
                &lt;?php
               </span>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-2">
               <span class="crayon-v">
                $chopped
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-h">
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-o">
                =
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-h">
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-e">
                rtrim
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-sy">
                (
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-s">
                'You really are the most interesting person in the world. cANyOUbELIEVEtHAT?'
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-sy">
                ,
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-h">
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-s">
                'cANyOUbELIEVEtHAT?'
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-sy">
                )
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-sy">
                ;
               </span>
              </div>
              <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-558b4d16d40f5365504017-3">
               <span class="crayon-k ">
                echo
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-h">
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-v">
                $chopped
               </span>
               <span class="crayon-sy">
                ;
               </span>
              </div>

               <span class="crayon-ta">
                ?&gt;
               </span>

          String

  <script>
   csbwfsCheckCookie();function csbwfsSetCookie(cname,cvalue,exdays) {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "expires=" + d.toGMTString();
    document.cookie = cname+"="+cvalue+"; "+expires;
}

function csbwfsGetCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(var i=0; i&lt;ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
        if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) {
            return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
        }
    }
    return "";
}

function csbwfsCheckCookie() {
    var button_status=csbwfsGetCookie("csbwfs_show_hide_status");
    if (button_status != "") {
        
    } else {
        csbwfsSetCookie("csbwfs_show_hide_status", "active",1);
    }
}
  </script>
